about_this_resource_text: '<p>This lecture and the next cover the role of natural
  language processing in machine learning in healthcare. In this lecture, Prof. Szolovits
  covers methods which are not based on neural networks representations.</p> <p>Speaker:
  Peter Szolovits</p>             <p><a href="./resolveuid/4690584c5836f89a2268ac33e6710b14">Lecture
  7: Natural Language Processing (NLP), Part 1 slides (PDF - 1.3MB)</a></p>'

  <span m="546330">5%</span> <span m="547170">corruption</span> <span m="548040">of</span>
  <span m="548190">that</span> <span m="548430">database,</span> <span m="549720">then</span>
  <span m="550020">we're</span> <span m="550170">going</span> <span m="550310">to</span>
  <span m="550410">get</span> <span m="550620">meaningless</span> <span m="551160">results</span>
  <span m="552090">from</span> <span m="552330">it.</span> <span m="553240">So</span>
  <span m="553440">that's</span> <span m="554130">the</span> <span m="554400">goal</span>
  <span m="554700">here.</span></p><p><span m="555720">So</span> <span m="555930">what</span>
  <span m="556140">we</span> <span m="556290">did</span> <span m="557850">is</span>
  <span m="558060">to</span> <span m="558180">say,</span> <span m="558580">well,</span>
  <span m="559690">if</span> <span m="559890">you</span> <span m="560730">train</span>
  <span m="562800">a</span> <span m="563000">data</span> <span m="563270">set</span>
  <span m="563700">that</span> <span m="564390">tries</span> <span m="564720">to</span>
  <span m="564870">tell</span> <span m="565170">you</span> <span m="565410">whether</span>
  <span m="565800">somebody</span> <span m="566340">really</span> <span m="566640">has</span>
  <span m="566910">rheumatoid</span> <span m="567420">arthritis</span> <span m="568020">or</span>
  <span m="568110">not</span> <span m="569010">based</span> <span m="569550">on</span>
  <span m="569880">just</span> <span m="570210">codified</span> <span m="570810">data.</span>
  <span m="571790">So</span> <span m="571980">codified</span> <span m="572550">data</span>
  <span m="572865">are</span> <span m="573180">things</span> <span m="573450">like</span>
  <span m="573690">lab</span> <span m="573930">values</span> <span m="574560">and</span>
  <span m="575070">prescriptions</span> <span m="575970">and</span> <span m="577020">demographics</span>
  <span m="578010">and</span> <span m="578250">stuff</span> <span m="578640">that</span>
  <span m="578990">is</span> <span m="579330">in</span> <span m="579510">tabular</span>
  <span m="580050">form.</span> <span m="581700">Then</span> <span m="582000">we</span>
  <span m="582180">were</span> <span m="582360">getting</span> <span m="583245">a</span>
  <span m="583590">positive</span> <span m="584160">predictive</span> <span m="584640">value</span>
  <span m="584970">of</span> <span m="585300">about</span> <span m="585690">88%.</span>
  <span m="587955">We</span> <span m="588420">said,</span> <span m="588720">well,</span>
  <span m="589320">how</span> <span m="590670">well</span> <span m="591030">could</span>
  <span m="591270">we</span> <span m="591450">do</span> <span m="592470">by,</span>
  <span m="593730">instead</span> <span m="594240">of</span> <span m="594390">looking</span>
  <span m="594990">at</span> <span m="595200">that</span> <span m="595410">codified</span>
  <span m="596070">data,</span> <span m="596460">looking</span> <span m="596910">at</span>
  <span m="597180">the</span> <span m="597450">narrative</span> <span m="597900">text</span>
  <span m="599010">in</span> <span m="599970">nursing</span> <span m="600420">notes,</span>
  <span m="600810">doctor's</span> <span m="601320">notes,</span> <span m="601680">discharge</span>
  <span m="602160">summaries,</span> <span m="602730">various</span> <span m="603180">other</span>
  <span m="603420">sources.</span> <span m="604620">Could</span> <span m="604830">we</span>
  <span m="604980">do</span> <span m="605400">as</span> <span m="605610">well</span>
  <span m="605880">or</span> <span m="606000">better?</span></p><p><span m="607020">And</span>
  <span m="607200">the</span> <span m="607320">answer</span> <span m="607710">turned</span>
  <span m="608070">out</span> <span m="608340">that</span> <span m="608580">we</span>
  <span m="609000">were</span> <span m="609210">getting</span> <span m="611220">about</span>
  <span m="612660">89%</span> <span m="614160">using</span> <span m="614670">only</span>
  <span m="615000">the</span> <span m="615150">natural</span> <span m="615570">language</span>
  <span m="615990">processing</span> <span m="616920">on</span> <span m="617100">these</span>
  <span m="617310">notes.</span> <span m="618810">And</span> <span m="618990">not</span>
  <span m="619230">surprisingly,</span> <span m="620100">when</span> <span m="620280">you</span>
  <span m="620400">put</span> <span m="620640">them</span> <span m="620790">together,</span>
  <span m="621900">the</span> <span m="622680">joint</span> <span m="623610">model</span>
  <span m="624270">gave</span> <span m="624600">us</span> <span m="624810">about</span>
  <span m="625140">94%.</span> <span m="627460">So</span> <span m="627670">that</span>
  <span m="627880">was</span> <span m="628180">definitely</span> <span m="628780">an</span>
  <span m="628900">improvement.</span></p><p><span m="630910">So</span> <span m="631390">this</span>
  <span m="632050">was</span> <span m="632290">published</span> <span m="632890">in</span>
  <span m="633850">2010,</span> <span m="635200">and</span> <span m="635350">so</span>
  <span m="635620">this</span> <span m="635860">is</span> <span m="636010">not</span>

  <span m="640390">results.</span> <span m="641920">But</span> <span m="642250">to</span>

  <span m="642970">very</span> <span m="643240">compelling</span> <span m="644020">story</span>

  <span m="2321680">does</span> <span m="2321950">reasonably</span> <span m="2322520">well.</span>
  <span m="2323760">So</span> <span m="2324500">if</span> <span m="2324710">you</span>
  <span m="2324890">look</span> <span m="2325340">at</span> <span m="2326030">sentences</span>
  <span m="2326840">that</span> <span m="2327110">do</span> <span m="2327290">not</span>
  <span m="2327920">contain</span> <span m="2328490">a</span> <span m="2328580">negation</span>
  <span m="2329630">phrase</span> <span m="2331200">and</span> <span m="2331370">looked</span>
  <span m="2331610">at</span> <span m="2331700">500</span> <span m="2332360">of</span>
  <span m="2332540">them,</span> <span m="2333450">you</span> <span m="2333500">find</span>
  <span m="2334100">that</span> <span m="2334430">you</span> <span m="2334550">get</span>
  <span m="2334760">a</span> <span m="2334820">sensitivity</span> <span m="2335570">and</span>
  <span m="2335690">specificity</span> <span m="2336620">of</span> <span m="2336790">88%</span>
  <span m="2337310">and</span> <span m="2337400">52%</span> <span m="2339520">for</span>
  <span m="2339980">those</span> <span m="2340430">that</span> <span m="2340670">don't</span>
  <span m="2341000">contain</span> <span m="2341720">one</span> <span m="2341960">of</span>
  <span m="2342080">these</span> <span m="2342320">phrases.</span> <span m="2343370">Of</span>
  <span m="2343490">course,</span> <span m="2343820">the</span> <span m="2343910">sensitivity</span>
  <span m="2344810">is</span> <span m="2344890">0</span> <span m="2345470">and</span>
  <span m="2345760">the</span> <span m="2346040">specificity</span> <span m="2346880">is</span>
  <span m="2347060">100%</span> <span m="2349460">on</span> <span m="2349880">the</span>
  <span m="2349970">baseline.</span></p><p><span m="2351300">And</span> <span m="2351380">if</span>
  <span m="2351530">you</span> <span m="2351740">use</span> <span m="2352100">NegEx,</span>
  <span m="2353000">what</span> <span m="2353300">you</span> <span m="2353420">find</span>
  <span m="2353900">is</span> <span m="2354170">that</span> <span m="2354410">you</span>
  <span m="2354530">can</span> <span m="2354890">significantly</span> <span m="2355940">improve</span>
  <span m="2356420">the</span> <span m="2356540">specificity</span> <span m="2358910">over</span>
  <span m="2359210">the</span> <span m="2359360">baseline.</span> <span m="2361000">All</span>
  <span m="2361080">right?</span> <span m="2362880">And</span> <span m="2363060">you</span>
  <span m="2363210">wind</span> <span m="2363540">up</span> <span m="2363750">with</span>
  <span m="2366250">a</span> <span m="2366810">better</span> <span m="2368040">result,</span>
  <span m="2369210">although</span> <span m="2369570">not</span> <span m="2369900">in</span>
  <span m="2370080">all</span> <span m="2370560">schemes.</span> <span m="2371310">So</span>
  <span m="2372030">what</span> <span m="2372240">this</span> <span m="2372450">means</span>
  <span m="2372870">is</span> <span m="2373020">that</span> <span m="2373200">very</span>
  <span m="2373470">simplistic</span> <span m="2374190">techniques</span> <span m="2375240">can</span>
  <span m="2375420">actually</span> <span m="2375900">work</span> <span m="2376230">reasonably</span>
  <span m="2376800">well</span> <span m="2377070">at</span> <span m="2377190">times.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2381420">generalization?</span> <span m="2382920">One</span> <span m="2383190">way</span>
  <span m="2383400">is</span> <span m="2383580">to</span> <span m="2383700">take</span>
  <span m="2384210">advantage</span> <span m="2384750">of</span> <span m="2384900">related</span>

  <span m="2391350">of</span> <span m="2391500">a</span> <span m="2391530">word.</span>
  <span m="2391920">You</span> <span m="2392040">might</span> <span m="2392280">look</span>
  <span m="2392490">for</span> <span m="2392670">those</span> <span m="2393660">other</span>
  <span m="2393930">associated</span> <span m="2394620">terms.</span> <span m="2395650">For</span>
  <span m="2395730">example,</span> <span m="2396550">if</span> <span m="2396660">you're</span>
  <span m="2397410">looking</span> <span m="2397860">to</span> <span m="2398010">see</span>
  <span m="2398280">whether</span> <span m="2398640">a</span> <span m="2398700">patient</span>
  <span m="2399150">has</span> <span m="2399390">a</span> <span m="2399480">certain</span>
  <span m="2399870">disease,</span> <span m="2400980">then</span> <span m="2401250">you</span>
  <span m="2401370">can</span> <span m="2401580">do</span> <span m="2401790">a</span>
  <span m="2401850">little</span> <span m="2402090">bit</span> <span m="2402270">of</span>
  <span m="2402360">diagnostic</span> <span m="2403140">reasoning</span> <span m="2403680">and</span>
  <span m="2403800">say,</span> <span m="2404610">if</span> <span m="2404790">I</span>
  <span m="2404940">see</span> <span m="2405210">a</span> <span m="2405270">lot</span>
  <span m="2405510">of</span> <span m="2405630">symptoms</span> <span m="2406260">of</span>
  <span m="2406380">that</span> <span m="2406650">disease</span> <span m="2407100">mentioned,</span>
  <span m="2408000">then</span> <span m="2408210">maybe</span> <span m="2408510">the</span>
  <span m="2408660">disease</span> <span m="2409090">is</span> <span m="2409260">present</span>
  <span m="2409770">as</span> <span m="2409950">well.</span></p><p><span m="2412200">So</span>
  <span m="2412860">the</span> <span m="2413070">recursive</span> <span m="2414240">machine</span>
  <span m="2414660">learning</span> <span m="2414990">problem</span> <span m="2415980">is</span>
  <span m="2416190">how</span> <span m="2416430">best</span> <span m="2416760">to</span>
  <span m="2416940">identify</span> <span m="2418320">the</span> <span m="2418620">things</span>

  <span m="2420210">term.</span> <span m="2420690">And</span> <span m="2420810">this</span>

  <span m="2429900">how</span> <span m="2430110">many</span> <span m="2430320">of</span>
  <span m="2430470">you</span> <span m="2430590">have</span> <span m="2430800">used</span>
  <span m="2431070">the</span> <span m="2431400">UMLS?</span> <span m="2433780">Just</span>

  <span m="2473780">it</span> <span m="2473870">does</span> <span m="2474200">include</span>
  <span m="2474770">all</span> <span m="2474980">of</span> <span m="2475100">this</span>
  <span m="2475280">terminology.</span></p><p><span m="2476810">And</span> <span m="2476960">then</span>
  <span m="2477110">they</span> <span m="2477260">spent</span> <span m="2477710">a</span>

  <span m="2558860">looking</span> <span m="2559220">for.</span></p><p><span m="2560790">So</span>

  <span m="2589510">created</span> <span m="2590650">a</span> <span m="2590710">semantic</span>
  <span m="2591280">network</span> <span m="2592390">that</span> <span m="2592660">says</span>

  <span m="2594640">relations</span> <span m="2595400">and</span> <span m="2595570">127</span>

  <span m="2599050">concept</span> <span m="2599650">unique</span> <span m="2600070">identifier</span>
  <span m="2601300">is</span> <span m="2601510">assigned</span> <span m="2601990">at</span>

  <span m="2603220">type.</span> <span m="2604060">So</span> <span m="2604240">this</span>

  <span m="2606610">this</span> <span m="2606760">stuff.</span></p><p><span m="2608560">Here</span>

  <span m="2619540">you</span> <span m="2619690">see</span> <span m="2619990">that</span>

  <span m="2625240">stands</span> <span m="2625660">for</span> <span m="2625840">therapeutic</span>
  <span m="2626560">or</span> <span m="2626710">preventive</span> <span m="2627280">procedure.</span>
  <span m="2628610">And</span> <span m="2628690">there</span> <span m="2628840">are</span>
  <span m="2628930">260,000</span> <span m="2630610">of</span> <span m="2630790">those</span>
  <span m="2631360">concepts</span> <span m="2632450">in</span> <span m="2633970">the</span>
  <span m="2634060">meta-thesaurus.</span> <span m="2635800">There</span> <span m="2636070">are</span>
  <span m="2637000">233,000</span> <span m="2638650">findings,</span> <span m="2639850">172,000</span>
  <span m="2641350">drugs,</span> <span m="2642400">organic</span> <span m="2642910">chemicals,</span>
  <span m="2643600">pharmacological</span> <span m="2644500">substances,</span> <span
  m="2646270">amino</span> <span m="2646660">acid</span> <span m="2646990">peptide</span>
  <span m="2647530">or</span> <span m="2647620">protein,</span> <span m="2648760">invertebrate.</span>
  <span m="2649960">So</span> <span m="2650140">the</span> <span m="2650500">data</span>
  <span m="2650950">does</span> <span m="2651220">not</span> <span m="2651490">come</span>
  <span m="2651790">only</span> <span m="2652090">from</span> <span m="2653140">human</span>
  <span m="2653500">medicine</span> <span m="2654070">but</span> <span m="2654250">also</span>
  <span m="2654640">from</span> <span m="2654940">veterinary</span> <span m="2655600">medicine</span>
  <span m="2656210">and</span> <span m="2656860">bioinformatics</span> <span m="2657880">research</span>
  <span m="2658450">and</span> <span m="2658570">all</span> <span m="2658750">over</span>
  <span m="2658960">the</span> <span m="2659050">place.</span></p><p><span m="2660310">But</span>
  <span m="2660580">you</span> <span m="2660700">see</span> <span m="2660970">that</span>
  <span m="2661180">these</span> <span m="2661510">are</span> <span m="2662040">a</span>
  <span m="2662170">useful</span> <span m="2662650">listing</span> <span m="2663640">of</span>
  <span m="2665920">appropriate</span> <span m="2669610">semantic</span> <span m="2670210">types</span>
  <span m="2670840">that</span> <span m="2671110">you</span> <span m="2671230">can</span>
  <span m="2671440">then</span> <span m="2671650">look</span> <span m="2671890">for</span>
  <span m="2672970">in</span> <span m="2673390">such</span> <span m="2673690">a</span>
  <span m="2673720">database.</span> <span m="2674950">And</span> <span m="2675070">the</span>
  <span m="2675160">types</span> <span m="2675640">are</span> <span m="2675730">hierarchically</span>
  <span m="2677050">organized.</span> <span m="2678820">So</span> <span m="2679090">for</span>
  <span m="2679300">example,</span> <span m="2681610">the</span> <span m="2681790">relations</span>
  <span m="2682570">are</span> <span m="2682720">organized</span> <span m="2683360">so</span>
  <span m="2683500">there's</span> <span m="2683770">an</span> <span m="2683890">effects</span>
  <span m="2684400">relation</span> <span m="2685540">which</span> <span m="2685780">has</span>
  <span m="2685990">sub-relations,</span> <span m="2687010">manages,</span> <span
  m="2687670">treats,</span> <span m="2688150">disrupts,</span> <span m="2689200">complicates,</span>
  <span m="2690070">interacts</span> <span m="2690760">with,</span> <span m="2691030">or</span>
  <span m="2691180">prevents.</span> <span m="2692980">Something</span> <span m="2693370">like</span>
  <span m="2693640">biological</span> <span m="2694450">function</span> <span m="2695020">can</span>
  <span m="2695320">be</span> <span m="2696030">a</span> <span m="2696100">physiologic</span>

  <span m="2697630">pathologic</span> <span m="2698410">function.</span> <span m="2699560">And</span>
  <span m="2699880">again,</span> <span m="2700540">each</span> <span m="2700780">of</span>
  <span m="2700900">these</span> <span m="2701170">has</span> <span m="2701350">subcategories.</span></p><p><span
